üîó ‚Ä¢ The Uttar Pradesh Public Service Commission (UPPSC) has announced the UPPSC GIC Lecturer Recruitment 2025 for a total of 1,518 vacancies in various Government Inter Colleges across the state. Union Bank SO (Wealth Manager) Vacancy 2025
üîó ‚Ä¢ Union Bank of India has announced the Wealth Manager Recruitment 2025 for 250 Specialist Officer (MMGS-II) vacancies. The post offers a pay scale of ‚Çπ64,820‚Äì‚Çπ93,960 plus allowances, with an approximate CTC of ‚Çπ21 lakh in Mumbai. Candidates must be between 25 and 35 years of age as on 1 August 2025, hold a full-time 2-year MBA/MMS/PGDBA/PGDBM/PGPM/PGDM from a recognized institution, and have at least 3 years of experience in Wealth Management at the Officer/Manager level. Desirable certifications include NISM, IRDAI, NCFM, or AMFI. The application process will be open from 5 August to 25 August 2025, with fees of ‚Çπ177 for SC/ST/PwBD candidates and ‚Çπ1,180 for others. The selection process may include an online examination, group discussion, and personal interview. Selected candidates will serve a probation period of 2 years and must sign a service bond to serve the bank for a minimum of 3 years or pay ‚Çπ2,50,000 plus taxes if leaving early.

Bank of Baroda Sales Manager & Agriculture Officer Vacancy 2025
üîó ‚Ä¢ Bank of Baroda has announced its Recruitment Drive 2025 for a total of 417 vacancies across two departments‚ÄîRetail Liabilities and Rural & Agri Banking. The available posts include Manager ‚Äì Sales, Officer ‚Äì Agriculture Sales, and Manager ‚Äì Agriculture Sales. The online application process begins on 6th August 2025 and closes on 26th August 2025. Candidates must hold relevant educational qualifications such as a graduation degree (with preference for MBA/PGDM in Sales/Marketing) or a 4-year degree in Agriculture-related fields. Prior work experience in sales or agri-sales (preferably in the BFSI sector) is mandatory. The selection process may include an online test, psychometric assessment, group discussion, and/or interview. Selected candidates will be posted anywhere in India and must commit to a 3-year service bond. Interested applicants are advised to visit the official Bank of Baroda website to read the full notification and apply online.

üîó ‚Ä¢ The Bihar Staff Selection Commission (BSSC) has released the official notification for the 4th Graduate Level Combined Competitive Examination 2025. This recruitment aims to fill 1481 vacancies across various departments of the Bihar Government. Candidates must be graduates, with specific subject qualifications required for certain posts. The online application process will be open from 18 August to 19 September 2025. The application fee is ‚Çπ540 for General/BC/EBC (male) and outside Bihar candidates, and ‚Çπ135 for SC/ST, women (Bihar residents), and PwD candidates. Interested and eligible candidates can apply through the official BSSC website at https://bssc.bihar.gov.in.

üîó ‚Ä¢ Samagra Shiksha, Chandigarh has released a notification for the recruitment of 218 Junior Basic Teacher (JBT) posts for Primary Classes (I to V). Candidates from across India are eligible to apply. The minimum qualification includes a Graduation degree from a recognized university, a 2-year Diploma in Elementary Education (D.El.Ed.) recognized by NCTE, and passing the CTET (Paper-I). The salary for the post is fixed at ‚Çπ45,260 per month. The application process is online and will begin on 07 August 2025 and end on 28 August 2025 (5:00 PM), while the last date to pay the fee is 30 August 2025 (2:00 PM). The application fee is ‚Çπ1000 for General/OBC/EWS, ‚Çπ500 for SC, and exempted for PWD candidates. The selection will be done through a written objective type test of 150 marks, with no interview. Category-wise distribution includes 111 posts for General, 44 for OBC, 41 for SC, and 22 for EWS candidates. Interested applicants must visit the official website ssachd.nic.in to apply and read the full notification.
MP Bhulekh (WebGis 2.0) 2025 - Khasra, B1, Naksha Download
üîó ‚Ä¢ MP Bhulekh (WebGis 2.0) 2025 is an official online portal developed by the Revenue Department of the Government of Madhya Pradesh. It allows citizens to access digital land records such as Khasra, B1, and Land Maps (Naksha) in PDF format. Through this platform, users can search by district, tehsil, village, or landowner name, and download digitally signed documents. The portal also provides an option to apply online for a Digital Land Ownership Certificate, ensuring transparency and easy access to verified land details. Services are available in both Hindi and English, making it citizen-friendly and accessible to all.
SBI Clerk (Junior Associate) Vacancy 2025
üîó ‚Ä¢ State Bank of India (SBI) has released the official notification for Junior Associate (Customer Support & Sales) recruitment under Advertisement No. CRPD/CR/2025-26/06. A total of 5583 vacancies have been announced, including 5180 regular and 403 backlog posts, to be filled across various states. The online application process will be open from 06 August to 26 August 2025. Candidates must hold a graduation degree in any discipline, with final year students also eligible to apply provisionally. The age limit is 20 to 28 years as on 01 April 2025, with age relaxation applicable as per government rules. The selection process includes an online Preliminary Exam, Main Exam, and a Local Language Proficiency Test (if applicable). The Preliminary exam is expected in September 2025, and the Main exam in November 2025. The starting basic salary is ‚Çπ26,730/-, with gross monthly emoluments of around ‚Çπ46,000/- in metro cities. The application fee is ‚Çπ750/- for General/OBC/EWS, while it is exempted for SC/ST/PwBD/Ex-servicemen. Selected candidates will be posted in the state/circle they apply for, and no inter-state transfer will be allowed. Interested candidates can apply online through the SBI official website: https://sbi.co.in/web/careers.
Bihar BSSC Office Attendant / Attendant (Special) Vacancy 2025
üîó ‚Ä¢ The Bihar Staff Selection Commission (BSSC) has released the official notification for the recruitment of Office Attendant / Attendant (Special) posts under advertisement number 06/25. A total of 3727 vacancies have been announced across multiple departments of the Bihar government. Candidates who have passed the 10th (Matric) examination from a recognized board are eligible to apply. The online application process will begin on 25th August 2025 and remain open until 26th September 2025. The selection will be done through a preliminary objective-type written examination, followed by a main exam for shortlisted candidates. The minimum age limit is 18 years, and the upper age limit varies by category, with applicable relaxations. Reservation benefits will be given as per Bihar government rules, including 35% horizontal reservation for women and 4% for PwD candidates. The recruitment offers a Level-1 pay scale, and candidates are advised to read the full notification before applying online through the official BSSC website: https://bssc.bihar.gov.in.

APAAR ID / ABC ID card Online Apply & Download
üîó ‚Ä¢ The Apaar ID (also called ABC ID) is a unique 12-digit identification number issued by the Ministry of Education, Government of India under the National Education Policy (NEP) 2020. It is designed for school and college students across India to digitally store their academic records, credits, and certificates. The card facilitates seamless credit transfer and academic mobility through platforms like DigiLocker and the Academic Bank of Credits (ABC Portal). Students can apply online using their Aadhaar and basic educational details. The card is available to all students from Class 1 onward and can be downloaded from DigiLocker or the ABC portal after registration.

üîó ‚Ä¢ MPPSC has released the Vehicle Transport Sub Inspector Recruitment 2025 notification. The recruitment aims to fill multiple SI posts under the Transport Department.
